I saw a review saying that it was a bit stingy. I was curious about how this five-star hotel could be so stingy. If it was because they didn't give us the choice when we checked in and chose the room, then it was indeed quite stingy. We hoped to stay in a room with a relatively good night view. After all, it was advertised as being in the Lujiazui Financial and Trade Center on the bank of the Huangpu River. But the front desk directly replied that there were no vacancies, but I observed in the corridor at night that there were still many unused rooms. The second was room service. I asked for things I needed, especially drinking water, twice, at 14:45 and around 10:30 the next morning. Both times it took nearly an hour to deliver it. I even woke up from the cold at night (the air conditioner in the room could not control the temperature). I asked for a quilt and the reply was no. I asked for a blanket or a bed sheet (we had two adults and one child, a king-size bed room, and one quilt for three people. There were no spare quilts and blankets in the room). That time was around 23:30. As a result, I sat in the room wrapped in clothes for an hour before it was delivered to me. The tickets included in the Ctrip order need to be asked for, otherwise they will not be given to you
Hygiene: The bedding is clean and tidy, but the towels have a strong odor and are yellow and black in color. The anti-slip mat is even more moldy. I don't pay much attention to the details of the hotel hygiene. It's OK as long as the places I touch and see are clean. But a five-star hotel can't even do the basic hygiene, which is a bit annoying.
Environmental, it is advertised that there are various activities and services during the Spring Festival, but I haven't seen them in reality. I went to the 24th floor to visit the executive lounge, but it was dark and creepy. The hotel is surrounded by high-rise buildings in Lujiazui, so there is no scenery outside the window (this is what the front desk told me, and there are petrochemical buildings and residential areas outside my window, and there is really nothing to see). The only scenery is the transparent atrium corridor, but it is outside the door, and you can only appreciate it when you go out for a walk or take the elevator.
The hotel hardware decoration is the standard InterContinental style. The deluxe room is only 30 square meters, and it has to fit a large bathroom and a 2-meter bed. You can imagine how cramped the space is.
The hotel lighting control system is relatively old, and there is no sense of civilization.
The buffet restaurant is not large, the ingredients are fresh, and you can see the foreign manager personally supervising and walking around and greeting guests. But no one collects the plates, and the desk service is not responsive in time.
In short, **'s recommendation is really not as good as **'s filming. If you don't come with the anchor who can create an atmosphere, it will be a completely different matter. For more than a thousand yuan a night, you can actually go to a more cost-effective and scenic hotel to enjoy it.
